2025-10-06 22:58:37,816 - INFO - 最终使用的主题上下文为: 'Anbennar: A Fantasy Total Conversion (This mod is "Anbennar", a fantasy total conversion mod. The following is a critical style guide and context briefing for the translation.  ## Core Theme & Setting The mod's central theme explores the pivotal question: **what happens after the age of sword and sorcery?** The setting is a classic, D&D-esque fantasy world (with elves, dwarves, orcs, mages) being violently thrust into the 19th-century Age of Industry. All translations must reflect this clash between a magical past and a technological future.  ## Tone & Style Guide The tone must shift **FROM** traditional high fantasy (like *D&D's Forgotten Realms*, *Dragon Age*) **TOWARDS** a more industrial, gritty, and magitech-infused Victorian fantasy style (like *Eberron*, *Dishonored*, or *Carnival Row*).  ## Key Thematic Conflicts -   **Magic vs. Technology:** The central struggle is between the "arcane elite" and the "democratizing power of technological artificery." -   **Fantasy Races in a Modern World:** The translation must consider how 19th-century challenges (nationalism, industrialisation, class struggle) uniquely affect traditional fantasy races. -   **Ideology & Inequality:** V3 themes of liberty and equality are complicated by a world with inherent magical and racial differences.  ## Critical Terminology -   **Artificery:** This is the key in-universe term for the new industrial technology that often blends magic and machinery. -   **Anbennar / Halann:** These are proper nouns for the world/continent and must not be translated. -   **Races:** Standard fantasy races (Elves, Dwarves, Halflings, Gnomes, Orcs) should be translated according to established conventions.)'
